     <p>
      <b>
       Edmund "Eddie" Irvine, Jr.
      </b>
      (born 10 November 1965) is a retired British
      <a href="/wiki/Auto_racing" title="Auto racing">
       racing driver
      </a>
      from
      <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">
       Northern Ireland
      </a>
      . He was the runner-up in 1999 Formula One World Drivers' Championship, driving for
      <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">
       Ferrari
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      Irvine was influenced by his parents to enter motor racing. He began his career at the age of seventeen when he entered the
      <a href="/wiki/Formula_Ford" title="Formula Ford">
       Formula Ford
      </a>
      Championship achieving early success, before progressing to the Formula Three and Formula 3000 Championships. He first drove in
      <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">
       Formula One
      </a>
      with the
      <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Grand_Prix" title="Jordan Grand Prix">
       Jordan
      </a>
      team in
      <a href="/wiki/1993_Formula_One_season" title="1993 Formula One season">
       1993 season
      </a>
      , where he achieved early notoriety for his involvement in incidents during his early career. He clinched his first podium finish in
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Formula_One_season" title="1995 Formula One season">
       1995
      </a>
      before moving to
      <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">
       Ferrari
      </a>
      in
      <a href="/wiki/1996_Formula_One_season" title="1996 Formula One season">
       1996
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      His most successful season was in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Formula_One_season" title="1999 Formula One season">
       1999
      </a>
      when he took four victories and challenged McLaren driver
      <a href="/wiki/Mika_H%C3%A4kkinen" title="Mika Hkkinen">
       Mika Hkkinen
      </a>
      for the World Championship, eventually finishing the runner-up. He moved to
      <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Racing" title="Jaguar Racing">
       Jaguar
      </a>
      in
      <a href="/wiki/2000_Formula_One_season" title="2000 Formula One season">
       2000
      </a>
      and endured poor results but managed to clinch his team's first podium in
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Formula_One_season" title="2001 Formula One season">
       2001
      </a>
      and another podium in
      <a href="/wiki/2002_Formula_One_season" title="2002 Formula One season">
       2002
      </a>
      . Irvine left Jaguar due to friction within his team and announced his retirement from competitive motorsport when he did not secure a race seat.
     </p>
     <p>
      Since leaving motorsport, Irvine became a media personality in Britain. He was also linked with the takeover of the Jordan and
      <a href="/wiki/Minardi" title="Minardi">
       Minardi
      </a>
      teams in 2005, with talks coming to nothing. Irvine also expanded his interests into the property market, having built up an investment during his racing career.
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>

         <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-23">
          <a href="#Complete_24_Hours_of_Le_Mans_results">
           <span class="tocnumber">
            6.4
           </span>
           <span class="toctext">
            Complete 24 Hours of Le Mans results
           </span>
          </a>
         </li>
         <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-24">
          <a href="#Complete_Formula_One_Grand_Prix_results">
           <span class="tocnumber">
            6.5
           </span>
           <span class="toctext">
            Complete Formula One Grand Prix results
           </span>
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </li>
       <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-25">
        <a href="#References">
         <span class="tocnumber">
          7
         </span>
         <span class="toctext">
          References
         </span>
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-26">
        <a href="#Bilography">
         <span class="tocnumber">
          8
         </span>
         <span class="toctext">
          Bilography
         </span>
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-27">
        <a href="#Further_reading">
         <span class="tocnumber">
          9
         </span>
         <span class="toctext">
          Further reading
         </span>
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-28">
        <a href="#External_links">
