       </li>
      </ul>
     </div>
     <p>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_and_career">
       Early life and career
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tleft">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irvine_89.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="495" data-file-width="705" height="154" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f9/Irvine_89.jpg/220px-Irvine_89.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f9/Irvine_89.jpg/330px-Irvine_89.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f9/Irvine_89.jpg/440px-Irvine_89.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Irvine_89.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Eddie Irvine at the 1989
        <a href="/wiki/Macau_Grand_Prix" title="Macau Grand Prix">
         Macau Grand Prix
        </a>
        . His helmet design was based on that of Ayrton Senna.
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Irvine was born on 10 November 1965 in
      <a href="/wiki/Newtownards" title="Newtownards">
       Newtownards
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/County_Down" title="County Down">
       County Down
      </a>
      in Northern Ireland, to Edmund Sr. and Kathleen. He spent his childhood in the village of
      <a href="/wiki/Conlig" title="Conlig">
       Conlig
      </a>
      . He has one older sister, Sonia who acted as Irvine's physiotherapist until 1999.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-1">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        1
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He completed studies in high school Regent House Grammar School, without ever excelling particularly in the results. Irvine's first taste of motorsport came when his family spent their holidays attending the
      <a href="/wiki/British_Grand_Prix" title="British Grand Prix">
       British Grand Prix
      </a>
      . His father also raced in single-seater cars for fun. Irvine originally expressed interest in motorcycles but his father thought them too dangerous. Irvine worked unpaid in his father's scrapyard, in return for which his father funded his racing hobby.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEIrvine.2C_Nottage2000102.E2.80.93103_2-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEIrvine.2C_Nottage2000102.E2.80.93103-2">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        2
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He later listed
      <a href="/wiki/John_Watson_(racing_driver)" title="John Watson (racing driver)">
       John Watson
      </a>
      as his childhood hero.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEIrvine.2C_Nottage200028_3-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEIrvine.2C_Nottage200028-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Irvine began to compete with racing cars in 1983, encouraged by his father;
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IrvineIniz_4-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-IrvineIniz-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine was initially interested in motorcycle racing, but his parents thought the sport too dangerous and so was forced to engage in the
      <a href="/wiki/Formula_Ford" title="Formula Ford">
       Formula Ford
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IrvineIniz_4-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-IrvineIniz-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      After participating in some races, in 1984 he won his first race at
      <a href="/wiki/Brands_Hatch" title="Brands Hatch">
       Brands Hatch
      </a>
      , occasion which also won the award for best pilot.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IrvineIniz_4-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-IrvineIniz-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In 1987, he signed a contract with the
      <a href="/wiki/Van_Diemen" title="Van Diemen">
       Van Diemen
      </a>
      team and in that year he managed to win the title of the category, the
      <a href="/wiki/Formula_Ford_Festival" title="Formula Ford Festival">
       Formula Ford Festival
      </a>
      and the RAC Formula Ford series.
     </p>
     <p>
      At the end of the season, he participated, during the winter, in a test organised by
      <a href="/wiki/Marlboro_(cigarette)" title="Marlboro (cigarette)">
       Marlboro
      </a>
      in which the winner would get a place in
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/British_Formula_Three" title="British Formula Three">
       British Formula Three
      </a>
      ; Irvine set the fastest time and ensured the participation in the championship series of the aforementioned automobile.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IrvineIniz2_5-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-IrvineIniz2-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      During this season not won any success and ended the season in fifth place. He also attended the
      <a href="/wiki/Macau_Grand_Prix" title="Macau Grand Prix">
       Macau Grand Prix
      </a>
      , part of the league schedule of
      <a href="/wiki/Formula_Three" title="Formula Three">
       Formula Three
      </a>
      , succeeding from the
      <a href="/wiki/Pole_position" title="Pole position">
       pole position
      </a>
      , but did not win the race. Thanks to Marlboro could also take part, the following year, the championship of
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/F3000" title="F3000">
       F3000
      </a>
      with the team
      <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Racing" title="Pacific Racing">
       Pacific Racing
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IrvineIniz2_5-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-IrvineIniz2-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Flanked by
      <a href="/wiki/JJ_Lehto" title="JJ Lehto">
       JJ Lehto
      </a>
      , considered then a young promise of motoring,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IrvineIniz2_5-2">
       <a href="#cite_note-IrvineIniz2-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      managed to finish in ninth place ahead of his teammate, thirteenth.
     </p>
     <p>
      In 1990 he signed a contract to race in Formula 3000 with the team
      <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Grand_Prix" title="Jordan Grand Prix">
       Jordan
      </a>
      . During the season, won a victory in Germany and ended the season in third place, with results better than his teammates
      <a href="/wiki/Heinz-Harald_Frentzen" title="Heinz-Harald Frentzen">
       Heinz-Harald Frentzen
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Emanuele_Naspetti" title="Emanuele Naspetti">
       Emanuele Naspetti
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">
       <a href="#cite_note-6">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        6
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      At year end, he took part again at
      <a href="/wiki/Macau_Grand_Prix" title="Macau Grand Prix">
       Macau Grand Prix
      </a>
      and the
      <i>
       Fuji F3 Cup
      </i>
      , finishing on the podium both races. The end of the season coincided, however, with the end of the relationship with the Irish team and Irvine moved to Japan to compete in
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Formula_Nippon" title="Formula Nippon">
       Formula Nippon
      </a>
      . During 1991, Irvine raced for
      <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Cerumo_Racing&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Cerumo Racing (page does not exist)">
       Cerumo Racing
      </a>
      where he clinched one victory with 17 points scored to finish seventh in the Drivers' Championship.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">
       <a href="#cite_note-7">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        7
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Irvine first appeared in the
      <a href="/wiki/1992_24_Hours_of_Le_Mans" title="1992 24 Hours of Le Mans">
       24 Hours of Le Mans
      </a>
      in 1992
      <a href="/wiki/SARD" title="SARD">
       SARD
      </a>
      driving a Toyota Group C car alongside
      <a href="/wiki/Roland_Ratzenberger" title="Roland Ratzenberger">
       Roland Ratzenberger
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Eje_Elgh" title="Eje Elgh">
       Eje Elgh
      </a>
      . The team finished ninth overall and came second in the Group C class.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">
       <a href="#cite_note-8">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        8
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Formula_One_career">
       Formula One career
      </span>
     </h2>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Jordan_.281993.E2.80.931995.29">
       Jordan (19931995)
      </span>
     </h3>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1993">
       1993
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Irvine entered
      <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">
       Formula One
      </a>
      , the highest category of circuit racing defined by the
      <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A9d%C3%A9ration_Internationale_de_l%27Automobile" title="Fdration Internationale de l'Automobile">
       Fdration Internationale de l'Automobile
      </a>
      (FIA), motorsport's world governing body, with the
      <a href="/wiki/Jordan_Grand_Prix" title="Jordan Grand Prix">
       Jordan
      </a>
      team, as team-mate to
      <a href="/wiki/Rubens_Barrichello" title="Rubens Barrichello">
       Rubens Barrichello
      </a>
      . Making his dbut at the
      <a href="/wiki/1993_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1993 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japanese Grand Prix
      </a>
      , Irvine finished in the points scoring positions with sixth place. He immediately became notable when he held up
      <a href="/wiki/McLaren" title="McLaren">
       McLaren
      </a>
      driver
      <a href="/wiki/Ayrton_Senna" title="Ayrton Senna">
       Ayrton Senna
      </a>
      for a number of laps. After the race, Senna walked into the Jordan motorhome and punched Irvine in the face.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">
       <a href="#cite_note-9">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        9
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine retired from the final race in
      <a href="/wiki/1993_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1993 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      when he suffered an accident.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">
       <a href="#cite_note-10">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        10
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Overall, Irvine finished 22nd in the Drivers' Championship scoring one point.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">
       <a href="#cite_note-11">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        11
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1994">
       1994
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Irvine remained at Jordan for
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Formula_One_season" title="1994 Formula One season">
       1994
      </a>
      and was again partnered by Barrichello. At the opening round in
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazil
      </a>
      , Irvine was involved in a four car pile-up. He later received a one-race ban and a $10,000 fine by the race stewards. Irvine appealed against the decision to the FIA who decided to reject the appeal on 6 April and increased the penalty to a three-race ban.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">
       <a href="#cite_note-12">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        12
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      His seat was filled by
      <a href="/wiki/Aguri_Suzuki" title="Aguri Suzuki">
       Aguri Suzuki
      </a>
      for the following
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Pacific_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Pacific Grand Prix">
       Pacific Grand Prix
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Andrea_de_Cesaris" title="Andrea de Cesaris">
       Andrea de Cesaris
      </a>
      for the races in
      <a href="/wiki/1994_San_Marino_Grand_Prix" title="1994 San Marino Grand Prix">
       San Marino
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Monaco_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Monaco Grand Prix">
       Monaco
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">
       <a href="#cite_note-13">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        13
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine returned for the
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Spanish_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Spanish Grand Prix">
       Spanish Grand Prix
      </a>
      where he scored his first points scoring position of the season with sixth place, although he suffered consecutive retirements in the following five races.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-irvine94_14-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-irvine94-14">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        14
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He was unable to finish the
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Belgian_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Belgian Grand Prix">
       Belgian Grand Prix
      </a>
      due to an alternator failure, although he was classified 13th due to having completed over 90% of the race distance; Irvine later did not finish the race held in
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Italian Grand Prix">
       Italy
      </a>
      due to an engine failure and was later given a one-race ban, suspended for three races for an first-lap incident with
      <a href="/wiki/Team_Lotus" title="Team Lotus">
       Lotus
      </a>
      driver
      <a href="/wiki/Johnny_Herbert" title="Johnny Herbert">
       Johnny Herbert
      </a>
      during the race.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">
       <a href="#cite_note-15">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        15
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Irvine garnered further controversy during the first qualifying session of the
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Portuguese_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Portuguese Grand Prix">
       Portuguese Grand Prix
      </a>
      when he clipped Williams driver
      <a href="/wiki/Damon_Hill" title="Damon Hill">
       Damon Hill
      </a>
      . Irvine was warned a similar incident would see his
      <a href="/wiki/FIA_Super_Licence" title="FIA Super Licence">
       Super Licence
      </a>
      revoked.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">
       <a href="#cite_note-16">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        16
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He finished seventh in the race and took consecutive points scoring finishes in the next two racesfourth at the
      <a href="/wiki/1994_European_Grand_Prix" title="1994 European Grand Prix">
       European Grand Prix
      </a>
      and fifth at the
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japanese Grand Prix
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-irvine94_14-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-irvine94-14">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        14
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine retired from the season closing race in
      <a href="/wiki/1994_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1994 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      when he spun off.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">
       <a href="#cite_note-17">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        17
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He finished the year 16th in the Drivers' Championship, with 6 points.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">
       <a href="#cite_note-18">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        18
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Outside of Formula One, Irvine participated in his third consecutive
      <a href="/wiki/1994_24_Hours_of_Le_Mans" title="1994 24 Hours of Le Mans">
       24 Hours of Le Mans
      </a>
      driving for
      <a href="/wiki/SARD" title="SARD">
       SARD
      </a>
      alongside
      <a href="/wiki/Mauro_Martini" title="Mauro Martini">
       Mauro Martini
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Krosnoff" title="Jeff Krosnoff">
       Jeff Krosnoff
      </a>
      . The team finished second overall and took victory in the LMP1/C90 class having led for 90 minutes and were forced to slow due to an gearbox issue.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">
       <a href="#cite_note-19">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        19
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1995">
       1995
      </span>
     </h4>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="217" data-file-width="495" height="96" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg/220px-Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg/330px-Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg/440px-Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Eddie_Irvine_1995_Britain.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Irvine driving for Jordan at the
        <a href="/wiki/1995_British_Grand_Prix" title="1995 British Grand Prix">
         1995 British Grand Prix
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Irvine remained at Jordan for
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Formula_One_season" title="1995 Formula One season">
       1995
      </a>
      and was again partnered by Barrichello. He endured a bad start: Irvine was forced into retirement at the opening race held in
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazil
      </a>
      due to an gearbox actuator problem,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">
       <a href="#cite_note-20">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        20
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and in the following race in
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Argentine_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Argentine Grand Prix">
       Argentina
      </a>
      , he made contact with McLaren driver
      <a href="/wiki/Mika_H%C3%A4kkinen" title="Mika Hkkinen">
       Mika Hkkinen
      </a>
      's left rear tyre and retired with an engine failure after six laps.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">
       <a href="#cite_note-21">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        21
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He managed to finish in eighth at the
      <a href="/wiki/1995_San_Marino_Grand_Prix" title="1995 San Marino Grand Prix">
       San Marino Grand Prix
      </a>
      and took his first points scoring finish by clinching fifth position in
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Spanish_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Spanish Grand Prix">
       Spain
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">
       <a href="#cite_note-22">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        22
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      After retiring from the
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Monaco_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Monaco Grand Prix">
       Monaco Grand Prix
      </a>
      , Irvine secured the first podium of his Formula One career with third place in
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Canadian Grand Prix">
       Canada
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">
       <a href="#cite_note-23">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        23
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Despite this success, Irvine did not score points in the following seven races. At the
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Belgian_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Belgian Grand Prix">
       Belgian Grand Prix
      </a>
      , Irvine's car caught fire during a pitstop as the fuel value was jammed open and was forced to retire.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">
       <a href="#cite_note-24">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        24
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In the week before the
      <a href="/wiki/1995_European_Grand_Prix" title="1995 European Grand Prix">
       European Grand Prix
      </a>
      , Jordan announced that Irvine would be retained on a two-year contract.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">
       <a href="#cite_note-25">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        25
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      However, Ferrari then announced that it had brought out Irvine's contract, and that he would be partnering
      <a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">
       Michael Schumacher
      </a>
      at the team for 1996.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">
       <a href="#cite_note-26">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        26
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He fared well in the race by finishing sixth, although he finished outside of the points in the
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Pacific_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Pacific Grand Prix">
       Pacific Grand Prix
      </a>
      . Irvine scored his final points of the season with a fifth in
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japan
      </a>
      and finished the season with a retirement due to pneumatic pressure in
      <a href="/wiki/1995_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1995 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-grandprix-australia_27-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-grandprix-australia-27">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        27
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He finished the year 12th in the Drivers' Championship with 10 points scored.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">
       <a href="#cite_note-28">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        28
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Ferrari_.281996.E2.80.931999.29">
       Ferrari (19961999)
      </span>
     </h3>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1996">
       1996
      </span>
     </h4>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_(cropped).jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1704" data-file-width="1260" height="298" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_%28cropped%29.jpg/220px-Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_%28cropped%29.jpg/330px-Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_%28cropped%29.jpg/440px-Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Michael_Schumacher-I%27m_the_man_(cropped).jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        <a href="/wiki/Michael_Schumacher" title="Michael Schumacher">
         Michael Schumacher
        </a>
        , Irvine's team-mate at Ferrari
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      At the first race in
      <a href="/wiki/1996_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1996 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      , Irvine clinched third position; in the following round held in
      <a href="/wiki/1996_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1996 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazil
      </a>
      , he finished outside of the points scoring positions with seventh position and took fifth in
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Argentine_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Argentine Grand Prix">
       Argentina
      </a>
      . At the
      <a href="/wiki/1996_European_Grand_Prix" title="1996 European Grand Prix">
       European Grand Prix
      </a>
      , he struggled with the handling of his car and was involved in an incident with
      <a href="/wiki/Olivier_Panis" title="Olivier Panis">
       Olivier Panis
      </a>
      causing both drivers to retire.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">
       <a href="#cite_note-29">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        29
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine took fourth in the
      <a href="/wiki/1996_San_Marino_Grand_Prix" title="1996 San Marino Grand Prix">
       San Marino Grand Prix
      </a>
      . However, Irvine endured with unreliability from his car and was forced to retire from the next eight consecutive races, due to being involved in incidents or problems with his car. The streak was ended when Irvine finished fifth in the
      <a href="/wiki/1996_Portuguese_Grand_Prix" title="1996 Portuguese Grand Prix">
       Portuguese Grand Prix
      </a>
      although he suffered another retirement at the season closing race in
      <a href="/wiki/1996_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1996 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japan
      </a>
      . Irvine finished tenth in the Drivers' Championship with 11 points.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">
       <a href="#cite_note-30">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        30
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1997">
       1997
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      The first race of the season in
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      saw Irvine involved in a crash with Williams driver
      <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Villeneuve" title="Jacques Villeneuve">
       Jacques Villeneuve
      </a>
      . The incident created controversy as it caused an rift with Irvine that lasted throughout the season. Irvine took 16th place at the next race held in
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazil
      </a>
      , having found his car difficult to drive, and secured an second-place finish in
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Argentine_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Argentine Grand Prix">
       Argentina
      </a>
      two weeks later where Irvine challenged Villeneuve for victory who was suffering from a stomach ailment and his car developed brake problems. The result had ended demands in the Italian press for Irvine's to be sacked. He maintained his form by clinching consecutive third place podium finishes in the following two races. This was cut short when Irvine retired from the
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Spanish_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Spanish Grand Prix">
       Spanish Grand Prix
      </a>
      where he garnered criticism from Panis and
      <a href="/wiki/Jean_Alesi" title="Jean Alesi">
       Jean Alesi
      </a>
      .
     </p>
     <p>
      At the next race held in
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Canadian Grand Prix">
       Canada
      </a>
      Irvine was involved in an incident alongside McLaren driver
      <a href="/wiki/Mika_H%C3%A4kkinen" title="Mika Hkkinen">
       Mika Hkkinen
      </a>
      on the first lap. He managed to recover by clinching another podium finish in
      <a href="/wiki/1997_French_Grand_Prix" title="1997 French Grand Prix">
       France
      </a>
      , although this was short lived as Irvine's form dipped when he finished outside of the points scoring positions in the following seven races. During the summer, it was announced that Irvine would remain at Ferrari for 1998.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">
       <a href="#cite_note-31">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        31
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      His run of poor results was ended with a third-place finish at the
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japanese Grand Prix
      </a>
      , and concluded the season with an fifth place at the
      <a href="/wiki/1997_European_Grand_Prix" title="1997 European Grand Prix">
       European Grand Prix
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">
       <a href="#cite_note-32">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        32
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine finished seventh in the Drivers' Championship with 24 points.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">
       <a href="#cite_note-33">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        33
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1998">
       1998
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Irvine remained at Ferrari for
      <a href="/wiki/1998_Formula_One_season" title="1998 Formula One season">
       1998
      </a>
      and was again partnered with Schumacher. Irvine's fitness level was placed in doubt when he suffered from back pain. To combat the issue, a new seat was installed in his car.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">
       <a href="#cite_note-34">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        34
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine had very little testing of his team's car, the
      <a href="/wiki/Ferrari_F300" title="Ferrari F300">
       Ferrari F300
      </a>
      , during pre-season testing and was concerned over the tyre war between
      <a href="/wiki/Bridgestone" title="Bridgestone">
       Bridgestone
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Goodyear_Tire_and_Rubber_Company" title="Goodyear Tire and Rubber Company">
       Goodyear
      </a>
      but was confident about his chances over the coming season.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">
       <a href="#cite_note-35">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        35
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      At the first race of the season in
      <a href="/wiki/1998_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1998 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      , Irvine finished in fourth and in the following race held in
      <a href="/wiki/1998_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1998 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazil
      </a>
      he clinched eighth position. After these results, Irvine endured a good half of the season as he finished on the podium six times in the next eight races, which included an retirement in
      <a href="/wiki/1998_Spanish_Grand_Prix" title="1998 Spanish Grand Prix">
       Spain
      </a>
      when he was involved in a collision with Benetton driver
      <a href="/wiki/Giancarlo_Fisichella" title="Giancarlo Fisichella">
       Giancarlo Fisichella
      </a>
      which created controversy. He managed to finish second place in
      <a href="/wiki/1998_French_Grand_Prix" title="1998 French Grand Prix">
       France
      </a>
      behind team-mate Schumacher which was the first one-two finish for Ferrari in eight years.
     </p>
     <p>
      In July, it was announced Irvine had signed an two-year extension to his contract.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-36">
       <a href="#cite_note-36">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        36
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The contract stipulated that Irvine was permitted to choose his own strategy and setup, although he would remain a supporting role to Schumacher.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">
       <a href="#cite_note-37">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        37
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      After two retirements in the next three races, Irvine recovered to finish second in
      <a href="/wiki/1998_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="1998 Italian Grand Prix">
       Italy
      </a>
      and secured fourth position at the
      <a href="/wiki/1998_Luxembourg_Grand_Prix" title="1998 Luxembourg Grand Prix">
       Luxembourg Grand Prix
      </a>
      . He closed off the season with a second-place finish in
      <a href="/wiki/1998_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1998 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japan
      </a>
      . Irvine finished the season fourth in the Drivers' Championship and scored 47 points.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">
       <a href="#cite_note-38">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        38
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="1999">
       1999
      </span>
     </h4>
     <div class="thumb tleft">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="479" data-file-width="640" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg/220px-Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg/330px-Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg/440px-Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Eddie_Irvine_1999_Canada.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Irvine driving for Ferrari at the
        <a href="/wiki/1999_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Canadian Grand Prix">
         1999 Canadian Grand Prix
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      For
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Formula_One_season" title="1999 Formula One season">
       1999
      </a>
      , Irvine was confident heading into the season, saying: "After last year's results where I got my best ever championship finish with 4th place overall, now, for this year, I want to do even better".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">
       <a href="#cite_note-39">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        39
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      His season got off to a good start: Irvine clinched his maiden Formula One victory at the season opening round in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      ;
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">
       <a href="#cite_note-40">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        40
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and in the following race in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazil
      </a>
      , he secured fifth position despite an unscheduled pitstop.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">
       <a href="#cite_note-41">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        41
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Three weeks later in the
      <a href="/wiki/1999_San_Marino_Grand_Prix" title="1999 San Marino Grand Prix">
       San Marino Grand Prix
      </a>
      , Irvine's car suffered an engine failure after 46 laps and lost the lead of the World Drivers' Championship to team-mate Schumacher. He managed to clinch his second podium finish of the season in the following round in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Monaco_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Monaco Grand Prix">
       Monaco
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">
       <a href="#cite_note-42">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        42
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine followed the result by clinching third place in the next round in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Canadian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Canadian Grand Prix">
       Canada
      </a>
      despite a collision with McLaren driver
      <a href="/wiki/David_Coulthard" title="David Coulthard">
       David Coulthard
      </a>
      and set the fastest lap.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">
       <a href="#cite_note-43">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        43
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      At the
      <a href="/wiki/1999_British_Grand_Prix" title="1999 British Grand Prix">
       British Grand Prix
      </a>
      where Irvine clinched second place, Schumacher crashed after going off the high-speed
      <i>
       Stowe Corner
      </i>
      when his car's rear brake failed, resulting in a broken leg.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">
       <a href="#cite_note-44">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        44
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine assumed the role as his team's lead driver and was partnered by Finnish driver
      <a href="/wiki/Mika_Salo" title="Mika Salo">
       Mika Salo
      </a>
      for the next six races. Nevertheless, Irvine clinched consecutive victories in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Austrian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Austrian Grand Prix">
       Austria
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/1999_German_Grand_Prix" title="1999 German Grand Prix">
       Germany
      </a>
      where he regained the lead of the Drivers' Championship.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-45">
       <a href="#cite_note-45">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        45
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and clinched a further podium finish in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Hungarian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Hungarian Grand Prix">
       Hungary
      </a>
      where he struggled with oversteer on his car.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">
       <a href="#cite_note-46">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        46
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      However, Irvine and Salo had complained about the lack of development with the team's car with Irvine threatening to leave Ferrari if his championship bid was not fully supported.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">
       <a href="#cite_note-47">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        47
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Nevertheless, Irvine clinched consecutive points scoring finishes in the next two racesfourth in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Belgian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Belgian Grand Prix">
       Belgium
      </a>
      and sixth in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Italian Grand Prix">
       Italy
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">
       <a href="#cite_note-48">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        48
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In September, it was announced that Irvine would move to the
      <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_Racing" title="Jaguar Racing">
       Jaguar
      </a>
      team which had purchased the
      <a href="/wiki/Stewart_Grand_Prix" title="Stewart Grand Prix">
       Stewart
      </a>
      team in June and would be partnered by
      <a href="/wiki/Johnny_Herbert" title="Johnny Herbert">
       Johnny Herbert
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-49">
       <a href="#cite_note-49">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        49
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine finished seventh in the
      <a href="/wiki/1999_European_Grand_Prix" title="1999 European Grand Prix">
       European Grand Prix
      </a>
      after enduring a 48-second pitstop as one of his wet weather tyres had been misplaced and was placed under pressure from rival Mika Hkkinen.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">
       <a href="#cite_note-50">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        50
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      At the penultimate round in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Malaysian Grand Prix">
       Malaysia
      </a>
      , Irvine clinched his fourth victory of the season although he and Schumacher were later disqualified as it was discovered their car's bargeboards did not comply to Formula One's technical regulations.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">
       <a href="#cite_note-51">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        51
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Ferrari appealed to the FIA which was heard on 22 October. The following day, it was announced that the Court of Appeal overturned the decision ensuring a last race showdown.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">
       <a href="#cite_note-52">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        52
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      At the season closing round in
      <a href="/wiki/1999_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="1999 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japan
      </a>
      , Irvine crashed out of qualifying and only managed to finish third in the race losing the Drivers' Championship to Hkkinen by 2 points. However Irvine's efforts during the season helped Ferrari to clinch their first Constructors' Championship in 16 years.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">
       <a href="#cite_note-53">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        53
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine was awarded the
      <a href="/wiki/Hawthorn_Memorial_Trophy" title="Hawthorn Memorial Trophy">
       Hawthorn Memorial Trophy
      </a>
      , an annual award given to the most successful British or Commonwealth driver in Formula One over the course of one season.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">
       <a href="#cite_note-54">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        54
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He was also named
      <a href="/wiki/Autosport" title="Autosport">
       Autosport
      </a>
      's British Competition Driver of the Year for 1999.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">
       <a href="#cite_note-55">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        55
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h3>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Jaguar_.282000.E2.80.932002.29">
       Jaguar (20002002)
      </span>
     </h3>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2000">
       2000
      </span>
     </h4>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg/220px-Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg/330px-Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg/440px-Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Jaguar_R1_2000.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        The
        <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_R1" title="Jaguar R1">
         Jaguar R1
        </a>
        driven by Irvine in 2000
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Former British racing driver
      <a href="/wiki/Stirling_Moss" title="Stirling Moss">
       Stirling Moss
      </a>
      aired doubts over Irvine's hopes to be a championship contender at Jaguar over the coming season.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-56">
       <a href="#cite_note-56">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        56
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Former British World Drivers' Champion
      <a href="/wiki/Jackie_Stewart" title="Jackie Stewart">
       Jackie Stewart
      </a>
      , said: "He really has come together. He's been in the shadow of a number one driver at Ferrari. I think it was time that he shed that shadow and went on to race for himself."
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-57">
       <a href="#cite_note-57">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        57
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine endured a torrid start: At the opening two races held in
      <a href="/wiki/2000_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/2000_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazil
      </a>
      , Irvine suffered consecutive retirements due to spinning out. However, he later managed to finish in the next three races, albeit outside of the points scoring positions. He retired from the
      <a href="/wiki/2000_European_Grand_Prix" title="2000 European Grand Prix">
       European Grand Prix
      </a>
      from a collision with Williams driver
      <a href="/wiki/Ralf_Schumacher" title="Ralf Schumacher">
       Ralf Schumacher
      </a>
      after spinning from being overtaken by Arrows driver
      <a href="/wiki/Jos_Verstappen" title="Jos Verstappen">
       Jos Verstappen
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">
       <a href="#cite_note-58">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        58
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      At the next race in
      <a href="/wiki/2000_Monaco_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Monaco Grand Prix">
       Monaco
      </a>
      , Irvine scored Jaguar's first points with fourth place.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">
       <a href="#cite_note-59">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        59
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      He was forced to withdraw from the
      <a href="/wiki/2000_Austrian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Austrian Grand Prix">
       Austrian Grand Prix
      </a>
      due to abdominal pains caused by a bout of
      <a href="/wiki/Appendicitis" title="Appendicitis">
       appendicitis
      </a>
      although he participated in the event's first free practice session. He was replaced by the team's test driver
      <a href="/wiki/Luciano_Burti" title="Luciano Burti">
       Luciano Burti
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">
       <a href="#cite_note-60">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        60
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine was passed fit for the
      <a href="/wiki/2000_German_Grand_Prix" title="2000 German Grand Prix">
       German Grand Prix
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61">
       <a href="#cite_note-61">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        61
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      where he secured tenth position despite a spin.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">
       <a href="#cite_note-62">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        62
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He was unable to score further points in the next five races, which included a retirement in
      <a href="/wiki/2000_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Italian Grand Prix">
       Italy
      </a>
      when he collided with Salo on the first lap.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">
       <a href="#cite_note-63">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        63
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He finished off the season by finishing the final three races which included a points scoring finish at the season closing
      <a href="/wiki/2000_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="2000 Malaysian Grand Prix">
       Malaysian Grand Prix
      </a>
      where he finished sixth.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64">
       <a href="#cite_note-64">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        64
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine finished the season 13th in the Drivers' Championship and scored four points.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">
       <a href="#cite_note-65">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        65
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Outside of Formula One, Irvine took part in the Belfast City Open and Direct Millennium Motorsport Festival driving a Jaguar sportscar to celebrate the marque's participation in the Tourist Trophy.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">
       <a href="#cite_note-66">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        66
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2001">
       2001
      </span>
     </h4>
     <p>
      Irvine remained at Jaguar for
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Formula_One_season" title="2001 Formula One season">
       2001
      </a>
      and was partnered by
      <a href="/wiki/Luciano_Burti" title="Luciano Burti">
       Luciano Burti
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">
       <a href="#cite_note-67">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        67
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Despite his vocal frustrations, Jaguar team principal
      <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Rahal" title="Bobby Rahal">
       Bobby Rahal
      </a>
      backed Irvine for the upcoming season, although Irvine was not confident citing his uncertainty about his team becoming competitive.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">
       <a href="#cite_note-68">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        68
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Rahal became concerned over Irvine's attitude when the team's car, the
      <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_R2" title="Jaguar R2">
       Jaguar R2
      </a>
      , was underperforming during pre-season testing.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">
       <a href="#cite_note-69">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        69
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine supported the view of being sacked at the end of the season if his performances did not satisfy the team.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">
       <a href="#cite_note-70">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        70
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine clinched 11th place in the first round in
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="2001 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      and failed to finish in the next four consecutive races.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71">
       <a href="#cite_note-71">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        71
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Before the
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Spanish_Grand_Prix" title="2001 Spanish Grand Prix">
       Spanish Grand Prix
      </a>
      , Burti left Jaguar to join the
      <a href="/wiki/Prost_Grand_Prix" title="Prost Grand Prix">
       Prost
      </a>
      team so Irvine was partnered with
      <a href="/wiki/Pedro_de_la_Rosa" title="Pedro de la Rosa">
       Pedro de la Rosa
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">
       <a href="#cite_note-72">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        72
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine managed to finish the
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Austrian_Grand_Prix" title="2001 Austrian Grand Prix">
       Austrian Grand Prix
      </a>
      in seventh position and took Jaguar's first podium finish with third place in the following round in
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Monaco_Grand_Prix" title="2001 Monaco Grand Prix">
       Monaco
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">
       <a href="#cite_note-73">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        73
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In June, it was confirmed at Irvine and de la Rosa would be retained by Jaguar for 2002.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">
       <a href="#cite_note-74">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        74
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Despite this success, Irvine failed to finish five of the next eight races. He suffered from a neck strain at a test session at
      <a href="/wiki/Silverstone_Circuit" title="Silverstone Circuit">
       Silverstone
      </a>
      and took time resting during the summer break.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">
       <a href="#cite_note-75">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        75
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      During this period, Rahal attempted to sell Irvine to the Jordan team with an additional $10million to Irvine's salary. Irvine rejected the contract as he wanted to help Jaguar become more competitive.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">
       <a href="#cite_note-76">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        76
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The contract, originally mooted by Rahal as a joke, led to his sacking and he was replaced by Austrian World Champion
      <a href="/wiki/Niki_Lauda" title="Niki Lauda">
       Niki Lauda
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">
       <a href="#cite_note-77">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        77
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      At the
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Belgian_Grand_Prix" title="2001 Belgian Grand Prix">
       Belgian Grand Prix
      </a>
      , Irvine was involved in a collision with Burti who was trying to overtake him. Burti crashed at over 240kph and absolved any blame placed upon Irvine.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">
       <a href="#cite_note-78">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        78
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine managed to clinch his final points of the season with fifth in the
      <a href="/wiki/2001_United_States_Grand_Prix" title="2001 United States Grand Prix">
       United States
      </a>
      and ended the season by retiring from the
      <a href="/wiki/2001_Japanese_Grand_Prix" title="2001 Japanese Grand Prix">
       Japanese Grand Prix
      </a>
      from a failure of his car's power generators on the fuel rig.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-79">
       <a href="#cite_note-79">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        79
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine finished the season 12th in the Drivers' Championship having scored six points.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">
       <a href="#cite_note-80">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        80
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h4>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="2002">
       2002
      </span>
     </h4>
     <div class="thumb tleft">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Eddie_Irvine_2002.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="229" data-file-width="300" height="168" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/84/Eddie_Irvine_2002.jpg/220px-Eddie_Irvine_2002.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/84/Eddie_Irvine_2002.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/84/Eddie_Irvine_2002.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Eddie_Irvine_2002.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Irvine driving for Jaguar at the
        <a href="/wiki/2002_United_States_Grand_Prix" title="2002 United States Grand Prix">
         2002 United States Grand Prix
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      Irvine remained at Jaguar for 2002 and was again partnered by de la Rosa. In preparation for the upcoming season, Irvine undertook a fitness examination and recorded a high score. However, he was cautious about his team's prospects going into the year, saying: "We've just got to wait and see what happens with this car, that's the question mark".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">
       <a href="#cite_note-81">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        81
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      At the opening round in
      <a href="/wiki/2002_Australian_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Australian Grand Prix">
       Australia
      </a>
      , Irvine finished fourth;
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">
       <a href="#cite_note-82">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        82
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and in the following race in
      <a href="/wiki/2002_Malaysian_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Malaysian Grand Prix">
       Malaysia
      </a>
      , he was forced to retire with an hydraulics problem.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">
       <a href="#cite_note-83">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        83
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine later managed to clinch seventh place in the
      <a href="/wiki/2002_Brazilian_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Brazilian Grand Prix">
       Brazilian Grand Prix
      </a>
      , before he suffered consecutive retirements in the next three races. He later finished the
      <a href="/wiki/2002_Monaco_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Monaco Grand Prix">
       Monaco Grand Prix
      </a>
      in ninth position, which was followed up with further consecutive retirements in the seven races. However, this marked a turning point as Irvine managed to finish in all of the remaining races. He was in the points scoring positions twice in this perioda sixth-place finish in
      <a href="/wiki/2002_Belgian_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Belgian Grand Prix">
       Belgium
      </a>
      and took his final career podium with third in
      <a href="/wiki/2002_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="2002 Italian Grand Prix">
       Italy
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">
       <a href="#cite_note-84">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        84
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He finished the season ninth in the Drivers' Championship, with eight points.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">
       <a href="#cite_note-85">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        85
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      During the season, friction developed between Irvine and his team due to his vocal frustration at the lack of development of his car. In an effort to retain Irvine, Jaguar offered him a $6million reduction in his salary, however no agreement was reached. He considered a return to his former team Jordan for the 2003 season, with no agreement reached due to the team's financial problems.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">
       <a href="#cite_note-86">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        86
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Irvine also denied rumours that he would move into either the
      <a href="/wiki/CART_World_Series" title="CART World Series">
       CART World Series
      </a>
      or the
      <a href="/wiki/IndyCar_Series" title="IndyCar Series">
       IndyCar Series
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">
       <a href="#cite_note-87">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        87
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Post-Formula_One_.282003.E2.80.93present.29">
       Post-Formula One (2003present)
      </span>
     </h2>
     <div class="thumb tright">
      <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">
       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg">
        <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2592" data-file-width="3888" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg/220px-1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg/330px-1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ce/1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg/440px-1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg 2x" width="220"/>
       </a>
       <div class="thumbcaption">
        <div class="magnify">
         <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:1978_Ferrari_312_T3.jpg" title="Enlarge">
         </a>
        </div>
        Irvine demonstrating a
        <a href="/wiki/Ferrari_312T" title="Ferrari 312T">
         Ferrari 312T
        </a>
        3 at the 2009
        <a href="/wiki/Goodwood_Festival_of_Speed" title="Goodwood Festival of Speed">
         Goodwood Festival of Speed
        </a>
        .
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
     <p>
      In 2002, Irvine successfully sued
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/TalkSport" title="TalkSport">
       TalkSport Radio
      </a>
      for "passing off" his image in a print advertisement, as if he had personally endorsed the station.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">
       <a href="#cite_note-88">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        88
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">
       <a href="#cite_note-89">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        89
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Eight years later, Irvine will front a half-hour programme on the station, the LG Grand Prix Show, alongside regular Sunday evening presenter
      <a href="/wiki/Andy_Goldstein" title="Andy Goldstein">
       Andy Goldstein
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">
       <a href="#cite_note-90">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        90
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      On 24 July 2003, Irvine was arrested after being caught driving a scooter over 30mph through Hyde Park without a licence or insurance. He was to be sentenced at Bow Street Magistrates but Irvine did not attend. An arrest warrant with bail was issued.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">
       <a href="#cite_note-91">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        91
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Irvine played himself in the 2004 comedy
      <i>
       The Prince and Me
      </i>
      , which starred
      <a href="/wiki/Julia_Stiles" title="Julia Stiles">
       Julia Stiles
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">
       <a href="#cite_note-92">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        92
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He is now executive producer of a film being produced about
      <a href="/wiki/Paddy_Mayne" title="Paddy Mayne">
       Paddy Mayne
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">
       <a href="#cite_note-93">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        93
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      In late 2006 he launched a new television programme on the
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sky_One" title="Sky One">
       Sky One
      </a>
      channel, with two teams of celebrity racing drivers competing against each other.
      <a href="/wiki/David_Coulthard" title="David Coulthard">
       David Coulthard
      </a>
      was captain and coach of the
      <i>
       girls
      </i>
      team, and Irvine of the
      <i>
       boys
      </i>
      . Ultimately, despite some impressive performances by both teams, Irvine's team won by some margin.
     </p>
     <p>
      In May 2005, Irvine was rumormed to be heading a consortium to buy the Jordan team and stated his interest of running the team.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">
       <a href="#cite_note-94">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        94
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He was later linked to a possible sale of the
      <a href="/wiki/Minardi" title="Minardi">
       Minardi
      </a>
      team and held talks with team principal
      <a href="/wiki/Paul_Stoddart" title="Paul Stoddart">
       Paul Stoddart
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">
       <a href="#cite_note-95">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        95
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      He was a millionaire through property investment before reaching Formula One. Outside of F1, Irvine is said to have built up a multi-million
      <a href="/wiki/Pound_sterling" title="Pound sterling">
       pound
      </a>
      property portfolio, owning around forty properties throughout the world. According to the
      <a href="/wiki/Sunday_Times_Rich_List" title="Sunday Times Rich List">
       Sunday Times Rich List
      </a>
      , published in April 2006, Irvine was the fifth richest person of Northern Ireland at that time, having increased his personal fortune to approximately 160million. He is also the owner of
      <i>
       Eddie Irvine Sports
      </i>
      , a
      <a href="/wiki/Snooker" title="Snooker">
       snooker
      </a>
      ,
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Billiards" title="Billiards">
       pool
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Kart_racing" title="Kart racing">
       kart racing
      </a>
      ,
      <a href="/wiki/Paintball" title="Paintball">
       paintballing
      </a>
      , and
      <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">
       football
      </a>
      facility in
      <a href="/wiki/Bangor,_County_Down" title="Bangor, County Down">
       Bangor
      </a>
      , close to his native Conlig.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">
       <a href="#cite_note-96">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        96
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      In May 2006, it was announced that Irvine would be one of the celebrities taking part in
      <a href="/wiki/ITV_(TV_network)" title="ITV (TV network)">
       ITV
      </a>
      's
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Soccer_Aid" title="Soccer Aid">
        Soccer Aid
       </a>
      </i>
      . In aid of
      <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">
       UNICEF
      </a>
      , this television show featured an England vs the rest of the world
      <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">
       football
      </a>
      match, with teams made up of a mix of celebrities and ex-professionals.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">
       <a href="#cite_note-97">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        97
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Unfortunately, he had to pull out because of a leg injury.
     </p>
     <p>
      On 9 January 2014, Irvine was sentenced to six months in prison after being found guilty of "mutual injury" following a brawl in a night club in
      <a href="/wiki/Milan" title="Milan">
       Milan
      </a>
      , Italy with Gabriele Moratti, son of former
      <a href="/wiki/Mayor_of_Milan" title="Mayor of Milan">
       mayor of Milan
      </a>
      <a href="/wiki/Letizia_Moratti" title="Letizia Moratti">
       Letizia Moratti
      </a>
      . Moratti's lawyer, Vincenzo Saponara, told the media that the sentence was likely to be suspended and that neither man would go to jail.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">
       <a href="#cite_note-98">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        98
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Nationality">
       Nationality
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      By virtue of being born in
      <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">
       Northern Ireland
      </a>
      , a
      <a href="/wiki/Constituent_country" title="Constituent country">
       constituent country
      </a>
      of the United Kingdom, Irvine was a British citizen throughout his career. He also held a racing licence issued by the National Sporting Authority of the
      <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">
       Republic of Ireland
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Indyflag_99-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Indyflag-99">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        99
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      (Drivers are not compelled to obtain their licence from their home country.) The FIA's International Sporting Regulations state that drivers competing in FIA World Championships shall compete under the nationality of their passport, rather than that of the National Sporting Authority that issued their racing licence, as is the case in other racing series.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">
       <a href="#cite_note-100">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        100
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      This situation created some confusion as to Irvine's nationality when he appeared at podium ceremonies in the Formula One World Championship. At his third podium, a second place for
      <a href="/wiki/Scuderia_Ferrari" title="Scuderia Ferrari">
       Ferrari
      </a>
      at the
      <a href="/wiki/1997_Argentine_Grand_Prix" title="1997 Argentine Grand Prix">
       1997 Argentine Grand Prix
      </a>
      , an Irish
      <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Ireland" title="Flag of Ireland">
       Tricolour
      </a>
      was mistakenly flown by the race organisers.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sunflag_101-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-Sunflag-101">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        101
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      This led to his family receiving threatening phone calls. Irvine then requested that at subsequent races, a politically neutral
      <a href="/wiki/Shamrock" title="Shamrock">
       shamrock
      </a>
      flag be flown, and the non-sectarian
      <a href="/wiki/Londonderry_Air" title="Londonderry Air">
       Londonderry Air
      </a>
      be played to mark a victory.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Indyflag_99-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-Indyflag-99">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        99
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      An FIA spokesman said:
     </p>
     <table class="cquote" role="presentation" style="margin:auto; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: auto;">
      <tr>
       <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px 10px;">
        
       </td>
       <td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">
        As far as we understand, Irvine has a British passport so the Union Jack should be raised. ... I understand he has a special flag, but our regulations do not allow this.
       </td>
       <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px 10px;">
        
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td class="cquotecite" colspan="3" style="border: none; padding-right: 4%">
        <p style="font-size: smaller; text-align: right;">
         <cite style="font-style: normal;">
          FIA spokesman Francesco Longanesi.
          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sunflag_101-1">
           <a href="#cite_note-Sunflag-101">
            <span>
             [
            </span>
            101
            <span>
             ]
            </span>
           </a>
          </sup>
         </cite>
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </table>
     <p>
      Irvine has self-identified as being Irish:
     </p>
     <table class="cquote" role="presentation" style="margin:auto; border-collapse: collapse; border: none; background-color: transparent; width: auto;">
      <tr>
       <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: top; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: left; padding: 10px 10px;">
        
       </td>
       <td style="vertical-align: top; border: none; padding: 4px 10px;">
        But at the end of the day, I'm Irish. I mean, I've got a British passport, but if you're from Ireland, north or south, you're Irish. And 'British' is. . . such a nondescript thing, isn't it?
       </td>
       <td style="width: 20px; vertical-align: bottom; border: none; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 40px; font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-weight: bold; line-height: .6em; text-align: right; padding: 10px 10px;">
        
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td class="cquotecite" colspan="3" style="border: none; padding-right: 4%">
        <p style="font-size: smaller; text-align: right;">
         <cite style="font-style: normal;">
          1995 interview.
          <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">
           <a href="#cite_note-102">
            <span>
             [
            </span>
            102
            <span>
             ]
            </span>
           </a>
          </sup>
         </cite>
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </table>
     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">
       Personal life
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      He became known for his flirting with various women, including
      <a href="/wiki/Pamela_Anderson" title="Pamela Anderson">
       Pamela Anderson
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">
       <a href="#cite_note-103">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        103
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Irvine named his biggest influence as his former girlfriend Maria Drummond whom he met at the Macau Grand Prix in 1988. The pair remained friends for a year, staying in regular contact and the relationship became deeper when Drummond split up from her boyfriend.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FOOTNOTEIrvine.2C_Nottage2000108-109_104-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-FOOTNOTEIrvine.2C_Nottage2000108-109-104">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        104
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      From the relationship Irvine has a daughter, Zoe.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">
       <a href="#cite_note-105">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        105
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He said that the birth of his daughter was the best moment of his life despite not being a natural lover of babies.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-interview_106-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-interview-106">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        106
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      Irvine is seen by many as a playboy in the mould of
      <a href="/wiki/James_Hunt" title="James Hunt">
       James Hunt
      </a>
      , in contrast to the sport's modern stars, who are seen as staid and less flamboyant. Irvine is also remembered for his tendency to speak his mind, often to the irritation of some. Despite this, Irvine does not consider himself to be a playboy stating his life is "90% work".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-interview_106-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-interview-106">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        106
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      He was nicknamed "Irv the Swerve" and later "Fast Eddie".
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">
       <a href="#cite_note-107">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        107
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <h2>
